His precious stones and jewels shine like thousand stars in the night sky..  A lost little friendâ€¦</p>

                                <header class="module-header">
        <h3 class="module-name">Our source of inspiration</h3>
    </header>
    <section class="module-body htmlSection">
        <div class="entry-content cf">
            <div style="text-align: justify;">
<div><a href="https://storage.ning.com/topology/rest/1.0/file/get/7157652062?profile=RESIZE_180x180" target="_self"><img class="align-left" src="https://storage.ning.com/topology/rest/1.0/file/get/7157652062?profile=RESIZE_180x180" width="96" /></a></div>
"Now we have got so many students and <a href="https://www.iskconcenters.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">so many temples</a> but I am <strong>fearful</strong> that if we expand too much in this way that we shall become weakened and gradually the whole thing will become lost. Just like milk. We may thin it more and more with water for cheating the customer, but in the end it will cease to be any longer milk. Better to boil the milk now very vigorously and make it thick and sweet, that is the best process. <em><strong>So let us concentrate on training our devotees</strong></em> very thoroughly in the knowledge of Krishna Consciousness from our <a href="https://ebooks.iskcondesiretree.info" target="_blank" rel="noopener">books</a>, from <a href="https://audio.iskcondesiretree.info/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">tapes</a>, and in so many ways instruct them in the right propositions." -&nbsp;<em>letter June 22, 1972 by</em> <span style="font-size: 12px;">His Divine Grace</span> <a href="https://gaudiyahistory.iskcondesiretree.com/a-c-bhaktivedanta-swami-prabhupada/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">A. C. Bhaktivedanta Swami Srila Prabhupada</a><span style="font-size: 12px;">, founder acharya of International Society for Krishna Consciousness (</span><a style="font-size: 12px;" href="https://iskconcenters.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">ISKCON</a><span style="font-size: 12px;">)</span></div>
<div style="text-align: justify;">
<div style="text-align: left;"><strong>Srila Prabhupada's special:</strong></div>
<div style="text-align: left;"><a href="https://harekrishnacalendar.com/everyday-with-srila-prabhupada/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Daily quotes</a>&nbsp;| &nbsp;<a href="https://vaishnavsongs.iskcondesiretree.com/a-c-bhaktivedanta-swami-prabhupada/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Vaishnava songs</a>&nbsp;|<br /> <a href="https://backtogodhead.in/category/author/a-c-bhaktivedanta-swami-prabhupada/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Back to Godhead articles</a>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a href="https://audio.iskcondesiretree.com/index.php?q=f&amp;f=%2F01_-_Srila_Prabhupada" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Audio</a>&nbsp;|</div>
<a href="https://images.iskcondesiretree.info/index.php?sfpg=MDItLUNvbG9yaW5nX0Jvb2tzLzAxLS1TcmlsYV9QcmFiaHVwYWRhLyoqKioqYzI0OGU2NjAxZWI4NjIxNzU2ZTU0YjM4ZTdiODdhZDU" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Coloring pages</a>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a href="https://comics.iskcondesiretree.info/index.php?q=f&amp;f=%2F01_-_For_children_-_PDF_format%2F02_-_Srila_Prabhupada_short_stories" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Short stories (Comics)</a></div>

<ul>

<li>07 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="https://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/pandava-nirjala-mahadvadashi-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Pandava Nirjala Mahadvadashi</a></li>
<li>09 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/panihati-cida-dahi-utsava-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Panihati Cida Dahi Utsava</a></li>
<li>11 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/snana-yatra-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Snana Yatra</a></li>
<li>11 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/disappearance-day-of-sri-mukunda-datta-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Disappearance Day of Sri Mukunda Datta</a></li>
<li>11 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/disappearance-day-of-sri-sridhara-pandita-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Disappearance Day of Sri Sridhara Pandita</a></li>
<li>12 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/disappearance-day-of-sri-syamananda-prabhu-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Disappearance Day of Sri Syamananda Prabhu</a></li>

<li>21 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/disappearance-day-of-sri-srivasa-pandita-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Disappearance Day of Sri Srivasa Pandita</a></li>

<li>25 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/disappearance-day-of-sri-gadadhara-pandita-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Disappearance Day of Sri Gadadhara Pandita</a></li>
<li>25 June 2025 -&nbsp;<a href="http://harekrishnacalendar.com/vaishnava-calendar/disappearance-day-of-srila-bhaktivinoda-thakura-2025/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Disappearance Day of Srila Bhaktivinoda Thakura</a></li>

    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        if (!window.dataLayerMain) {
            return;
        }
        var handler = function (event) {
            var element = event.currentTarget;
            if (element.hasAttribute('data-track-disable')) {
                return;
            }
            var options = JSON.parse(element.getAttribute('data-track'));
            window.dataLayerMain.push({
                'event'         : 'trackEvent',
                'eventType'     : 'googleAnalyticsNetwork',
                'eventCategory' : options && options.category || '',
                'eventAction'   : options && options.action || '',
                'eventLabel'    : options && options.label || '',
                'eventValue'    : options && options.value || ''
            });
            if (options && options.ga4) {
                window.dataLayerMain.push(options.ga4);
            }
        };
        var elements = document.querySelectorAll('[data-track]');
        for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
            elements[i].addEventListener('click', handler);
        }
    });
</script>
